CASEFOLDING#

import re
def casefolding(abstrak):
    abstrak = abstrak.lower()
    abstrak = abstrak.strip()
    abstrak = re.sub(r'[?|$|.|!_:")(-+]', '',abstrak)
    return abstrak
df["Abstrak"] = df["Abstrak"].apply(casefolding)

def token(abstrak):
    nstr = abstrak.split(' ')
    dat = [] 
    for i, s in enumerate(nstr):
        if len(s) > 0:
            dat.append(i)
    new_nstr = list(filter(lambda x: x != '', [nstr[i] for i in dat]))
    return new_nstr

df["Abstrak"] = df["Abstrak"].apply(token)

def stopword_removal(abstrak):
    filtering = stopwords.words('indonesian')
    data = [x for x in abstrak if x and x not in filtering]
    return data
df["Abstrak"] = df["Abstrak"].apply(stopword_removal)

from sklearn.pipeline import Pipeline
from Sastrawi.Stemmer.StemmerFactory import StemmerFactory
def stemming(abstrak):
    factory = StemmerFactory()
    stemmer = factory.create_stemmer()
    do = []
    for w in abstrak:
        dt = stemmer.stem(w)
        do.append(dt)
    d_clean=[]
    d_clean= " ".join(do)
    print (d_clean)
    return d_clean
df["Abstrak"] = df["Abstrak"].apply(stemming)
